# Implement chat archival sync

## User
**Timestamp:** 2026-07-16T22:28:13.644Z

Implement a permanent, reliable project-conversation archival and synchronization system for this repository.

# Primary Objective

Create a system that stores all conversations related specifically to this project inside the GitHub repository under:

`Codex_Chats/`

The archive must be updated every time Codex finishes a task or prompt in this repository.

The system must:

1. Add project-related conversations that have never been archived.
2. Update conversations already archived when new messages have been added.
3. Skip conversations whose contents have not changed.
4. Never create duplicate conversation files.
5. Never archive unrelated conversations.
6. Never create an empty Git commit when nothing changed.
7. Commit and push transcript updates to GitHub safely.
8. Never overwrite, discard, stage, or commit unrelated working-tree changes.
9. Never claim a conversation was archived unless it was actually obtained from an accessible source and written successfully.

Do not build a superficial placeholder. Implement, test, document, and validate the complete workflow.

# Critical Source-Access Requirement

First inspect the repository, Codex environment, local workspace, available APIs, session metadata, configuration files, and accessible transcript storage to determine which conversation sources are legitimately available.

Possible sources may include:

* The current Codex task/session transcript.
* Previous Codex sessions associated with this repository.
* Project-local transcript files.
* A user-provided ChatGPT data export containing `conversations.json`.
* Numbered ChatGPT conversation JSON files from a larger export.
* Explicitly supplied Markdown, JSON, or text transcript files.
* Any supported project/session history source exposed directly by the Codex environment.

Do not:

* Scrape browser cookies.
* Extract login tokens.
* read protected browser credential databases.
* bypass ChatGPT access controls.
* fabricate missing transcripts.
* pretend Codex has access to ChatGPT Project conversations when it does not.
* archive summarized memories as though they were exact transcripts.

If direct access to live ChatGPT Project conversations is unavailable, implement a clean import-and-sync fallback for user-provided ChatGPT exports.

The system should operate automatically for accessible Codex sessions and incrementally whenever a newer ChatGPT export is placed in the configured import location.

# Required Directory Structure

Create a structure similar to:

```text
Codex_Chats/
├── README.md
├── manifest.json
├── chats/
│   ├── <stable-conversation-id>--<readable-title>.md
│   └── ...
├── imports/
│   ├── README.md
│   └── .gitkeep
├── reports/
│   └── latest-sync-report.json
└── schema/
    └── manifest.schema.json

scripts/
├── sync_codex_chats.py
├── sync_codex_chats.ps1
└── tests/
    └── test_sync_codex_chats.py

.codex/
└── chat-sync.json
```

Adjust the structure only where the existing repository architecture makes another arrangement clearly better.

Do not store an unnecessary second raw copy of every transcript unless there is a strong technical reason. The normalized Markdown files and manifest should normally be sufficient.

# Configuration

Create a version-controlled configuration file at:

`.codex/chat-sync.json`

It should support fields similar to:

```json
{
  "enabled": true,
  "archive_directory": "Codex_Chats",
  "project_names": [],
  "project_identifiers": [],
  "project_keywords": [],
  "repository_identifiers": [],
  "import_directories": [
    "Codex_Chats/imports"
  ],
  "automatic_push": true,
  "remote": "origin",
  "branch_strategy": "current",
  "redact_secrets": true,
  "include_tool_output": true,
  "include_reasoning": false,
  "preserve_deleted_conversations": true
}
```

Populate project identifiers based on the actual repository and project context discovered during implementation.

The system must not depend solely on broad keyword matching. Project filtering should use the strongest available evidence, in this approximate order:

1. Explicit project ID or repository association.
2. Exact project name.
3. Workspace or repository path association.
4. Transcript metadata.
5. Explicitly configured project tags.
6. Carefully evaluated keyword matching as a fallback.

A generic mention of pirates, Sea of Thieves, websites, PDFs, images, Codex, Sera, or treasure must not automatically qualify an unrelated conversation.

# Stable Conversation Identity

Every conversation must have a stable identity.

Prefer the original conversation or session ID supplied by the transcript source.

If no source ID exists, generate a deterministic ID using stable source metadata, such as:

* source type
* original file identifier
* creation timestamp
* first user-message hash

Do not use the current time as the sole identity input.

Renaming a conversation title must not create a duplicate file.

The manifest must remain authoritative for mapping stable conversation IDs to archive files.

# Manifest Requirements

Create:

`Codex_Chats/manifest.json`

Use a documented and validated structure.

Each conversation record should contain at least:

```json
{
  "conversation_id": "stable-source-id",
  "source_type": "codex_session",
  "source_identifier": "original-source-reference",
  "project_identifier": "resolved-project-id",
  "title": "Conversation title",
  "archive_path": "Codex_Chats/chats/stable-id--title.md",
  "created_at": "ISO-8601 timestamp",
  "updated_at": "ISO-8601 timestamp",
  "first_archived_at": "ISO-8601 timestamp",
  "last_synchronized_at": "ISO-8601 timestamp",
  "message_count": 0,
  "content_sha256": "normalized-content-hash",
  "source_sha256": "source-content-hash",
  "status": "active",
  "redactions": 0
}
```

The manifest must also contain:

* schema version
* synchronizer version
* project identity
* last successful synchronization time
* total conversation count
* total message count
* source coverage information
* warnings from the latest synchronization
* enough information to support future migrations

Write manifest updates atomically so an interrupted synchronization cannot corrupt the archive.

# Markdown Conversation Format

Store each conversation as readable Markdown.

Use YAML front matter similar to:

```yaml
---
conversation_id: "stable-source-id"
title: "Conversation title"
project: "Project name"
source_type: "codex_session"
created_at: "2026-07-16T12:00:00-04:00"
updated_at: "2026-07-16T17:00:00-04:00"
message_count: 24
content_sha256: "..."
archived_at: "..."
---
```

Then format messages chronologically:

```markdown
# Conversation Title

## User
**Timestamp:** 2026-07-16 12:00 EDT

Message contents...

## Assistant
**Timestamp:** 2026-07-16 12:01 EDT

Response contents...
```

Requirements:

* Preserve message order.
* Preserve headings, code blocks, lists, and links.
* Preserve image or attachment references when metadata is available.
* Record attachment filenames and types.
* Do not invent attachment contents.
* Clearly label tool calls and tool results when included.
* Do not include private model chain-of-thought or hidden reasoning.
* Preserve ordinary visible assistant explanations and status updates.
* Normalize insignificant formatting differences before hashing.
* Use UTF-8.
* Use deterministic line endings.
* Prevent malformed transcript data from breaking Markdown structure.

# Update and Deduplication Logic

For each discovered eligible conversation:

1. Resolve its stable conversation ID.
2. Locate its manifest record.
3. Normalize its visible contents deterministically.
4. Calculate a SHA-256 content hash.
5. Compare it with the stored hash.
6. If no record exists, create the conversation file.
7. If the hash changed, update the existing conversation file.
8. If the hash is unchanged, do not rewrite the file.
9. Update manifest synchronization metadata appropriately.
10. Do not treat a title-only filename difference as a new conversation.

When a title changes:

* Keep the same conversation identity.
* Either retain the existing path or safely rename it.
* Update the manifest.
* Avoid leaving duplicate files.
* Preserve useful Git history where practical.

When a previously archived conversation is absent from a later import:

* Do not delete it automatically.
* Retain the archive.
* Mark it as unavailable, missing from source, or archived only when there is reliable evidence.
* Do not infer deletion from a partial export.

# ChatGPT Export Importer

Implement support for official ChatGPT export formats, including:

* `conversations.json`
* Numbered conversation JSON files
* An extracted export directory
* A ZIP file when safely readable without destructive extraction

The importer must:

* Stream or incrementally parse large exports where practical.
* Avoid loading enormous files into memory unnecessarily.
* Resolve conversation IDs from export metadata.
* Extract visible user and assistant messages in correct order.
* Handle alternate message tree branches deterministically.
* Document how the selected active branch is resolved.
* Ignore conversations unrelated to this project.
* Update previously archived conversations when the new export contains additional messages.
* Avoid duplicating previously imported messages.
* Record the source export timestamp and hash.
* Never commit the original full-account export.
* Ensure `Codex_Chats/imports/` is configured so personal raw exports are ignored by Git except for documentation and `.gitkeep`.

Add appropriate entries to `.gitignore`, including raw exports, ZIP files, temporary extraction directories, locks, and local synchronization caches.

# Project Classification

Implement a transparent project-classification process.

For every candidate conversation, determine:

* Included
* Excluded
* Ambiguous

Automatically archive only conversations classified as included with sufficiently strong evidence.

Do not archive ambiguous conversations silently.

Record ambiguous candidates in the synchronization report with:

* conversation ID
* title
* timestamps
* classification evidence
* reason for ambiguity

Support a configuration override where a conversation ID can be explicitly included or excluded.

Example:

```json
{
  "include_conversation_ids": [],
  "exclude_conversation_ids": []
}
```

# Secret and Privacy Protection

Before writing or committing transcripts, scan newly added or changed content for likely:

* API keys
* access tokens
* passwords
* private keys
* session cookies
* database connection strings containing passwords
* GitHub personal-access tokens
* bearer tokens
* secret environment-variable values

Do not indiscriminately censor normal design details, names, story content, code, or repository paths.

Use explicit placeholders such as:

`[REDACTED: POSSIBLE API TOKEN]`

Record the count and category of redactions without storing the original secret in logs.

If confidence is low, stop automatic pushing for that synchronization and report the suspected secret rather than risking publication.

Never store secret values in:

* logs
* reports
* exception traces
* manifest fields
* test snapshots

# Synchronization Commands

Provide a Python command such as:

```powershell
python scripts/sync_codex_chats.py
```

Support:

```powershell
python scripts/sync_codex_chats.py --dry-run
python scripts/sync_codex_chats.py --verbose
python scripts/sync_codex_chats.py --no-push
python scripts/sync_codex_chats.py --source <path>
python scripts/sync_codex_chats.py --report-only
```

Create a PowerShell wrapper suitable for this Windows development environment.

The wrapper must:

* resolve the repository root correctly
* use the project virtual environment when available
* provide clear error output
* preserve the underlying process exit code
* work when invoked from directories other than the repository root

# End-of-Prompt Integration

Make transcript synchronization a mandatory Codex finalization step for work performed in this repository.

Inspect the existing `AGENTS.md`, repository instructions, Codex configuration, task runners, and available completion-hook mechanisms.

Add the requirement without deleting or weakening existing instructions.

The finalization workflow should be:

1. Finish the requested project work.
2. Run appropriate tests for that work.
3. Capture or ingest the latest accessible conversation/session data.
4. Run the chat synchronizer.
5. Verify the manifest and changed transcript files.
6. Run chat-sync tests or integrity validation.
7. Determine whether transcript files actually changed.
8. Commit and push chat changes only when appropriate.
9. Report the synchronization result in the final task summary.

Do not rely exclusively on a Git `post-commit` hook because prompts can finish without a code commit.

Where the Codex host exposes a legitimate task-completion hook, integrate the synchronizer there.

Where no reliable completion hook exists, make the `AGENTS.md` finalization instruction authoritative and provide an optional project task wrapper that runs synchronization before Codex reports completion.

The final Codex task response should contain a concise line similar to one of these:

```text
Chat archive: 2 conversations added, 1 updated, 14 unchanged; committed and pushed.
```

```text
Chat archive: no transcript changes detected; no archive commit created.
```

```text
Chat archive: synchronization completed locally, but push was blocked because a possible secret was detected.
```

Never report success merely because the script was invoked. Confirm its exit status, resulting files, Git state, and push result.

# Git Behavior

The transcript synchronizer must be extremely conservative with Git.

It must:

* Detect the repository root.
* Detect the current branch.
* Verify the configured remote.
* Fetch remote state before pushing.
* Never force-push.
* Never reset, clean, stash, checkout, or discard unrelated changes.
* Never stage the entire repository with `git add .`.
* Stage only files intentionally created or changed by the chat archive system.
* Preserve unrelated staged and unstaged changes.
* Detect merge or rebase states and avoid unsafe automation.
* Use a lock to prevent concurrent synchronizations.
* stop clearly when the remote branch cannot be updated safely.
* retry only safe transient failures.
* provide useful recovery instructions without modifying unrelated work.

Use a commit message such as:

```text
docs(chats): synchronize project conversations
```

If the main Codex task already includes an intentional commit and the transcript changes logically belong with it, the transcript files may be included in that commit.

Otherwise, create a separate transcript-only commit.

Do not create a commit when:

* no transcript content changed
* only a local synchronization timestamp changed
* the only difference is nondeterministic output
* synchronization failed
* the source was incomplete or untrusted
* possible secrets require review

Avoid rewriting `last_synchronized_at` in tracked files when no substantive transcript data changed. Otherwise every run would create meaningless Git noise, because humanity already has enough meaningless Git noise.

# Atomicity and Reliability

Implement:

* atomic temporary-file replacement
* UTF-8 validation
* deterministic serialization
* file locking
* rollback of incomplete archive writes
* clear nonzero exit codes
* structured synchronization reports
* idempotent repeated execution

If a crash occurs midway:

* existing valid transcript files must remain valid
* the manifest must remain valid
* a subsequent run must recover safely
* partially written temporary files must not be treated as archived conversations

# Reporting

Create:

`Codex_Chats/reports/latest-sync-report.json`

The report should include:

* synchronization start and finish time
* source types inspected
* source coverage
* conversations discovered
* included
* excluded
* ambiguous
* added
* updated
* renamed
* unchanged
* unavailable
* redacted
* failed
* files changed
* commit created
* commit hash
* push attempted
* push result
* warnings
* errors

Avoid changing the tracked report when it contains no substantive new information. Put highly volatile local execution diagnostics in an ignored cache or log instead.

# README Documentation

Create a useful `Codex_Chats/README.md` explaining:

* why the archive exists
* what sources are supported
* the limitation regarding inaccessible ChatGPT Project conversations
* how automatic Codex-session synchronization works
* how to request and import a ChatGPT data export
* where to place `conversations.json` or the export ZIP
* how conversations are filtered to this project
* how updates and deduplication work
* how hashes and stable IDs work
* how secret redaction works
* how to run a dry run
* how to inspect ambiguous classifications
* how automatic commits and pushes behave
* how to disable automatic pushing
* how to recover from a failed synchronization

Do not describe functionality that has not actually been implemented and verified.

# Tests

Add meaningful automated tests covering at least:

1. First import creates a conversation.
2. Reimporting the identical source makes no tracked changes.
3. Adding a new message updates the existing file.
4. A changed title does not duplicate the conversation.
5. Two different conversations with the same title remain separate.
6. Unrelated conversations are excluded.
7. Ambiguous conversations are reported but not archived.
8. Explicit include overrides work.
9. Explicit exclude overrides work.
10. Sensitive values are redacted or block pushing.
11. Partial exports do not delete archived conversations.
12. Corrupt source files fail safely.
13. Interrupted writes do not corrupt the manifest.
14. Existing unrelated Git changes are untouched.
15. Nothing is committed when hashes are unchanged.
16. Windows paths and Unicode titles work.
17. Duplicate source records are reconciled deterministically.
18. Multiple synchronization runs are idempotent.
19. Concurrent runs are locked safely.
20. Manifest schema validation succeeds.

Use sanitized fixtures. Never place real account exports or secrets in the test suite.

# Initial Backfill

After implementation:

1. Discover all legitimately accessible conversations associated with this project.
2. Run a dry-run synchronization.
3. Review classification results.
4. Perform the initial archive synchronization.
5. Validate every generated transcript.
6. Confirm unrelated conversations were excluded.
7. Confirm rerunning synchronization produces no transcript changes.
8. Commit and push the implementation and initial archive, provided no secrets or unsafe Git conditions are present.

If only the current Codex session is available, archive only that session and report the exact limitation.

Do not create fake historical conversation files based on summaries or assumptions.

# Required Validation

Before declaring completion, verify:

* Every archived conversation has exactly one manifest entry.
* Every active manifest entry points to an existing file.
* Every transcript hash matches its file contents.
* Conversation IDs are unique.
* Archive filenames are portable across Windows and Linux.
* Raw account-export files are ignored by Git.
* No likely secrets remain in tracked archive files.
* An unchanged second run produces a clean Git diff.
* Existing unrelated working-tree changes remain untouched.
* The commit exists locally when one was required.
* The remote branch contains the pushed commit when automatic pushing was required and permitted.

# Completion Report

Return a detailed implementation report including:

* source-access capabilities discovered
* exact files created and changed
* project-classification method
* archive format
* initial conversation counts
* added, updated, unchanged, excluded, and ambiguous counts
* tests executed and results
* secret-scan results
* first-run and second-run idempotency results
* Git commit hash
* branch
* push result
* any remaining limitation preventing automatic access to ChatGPT Project conversations

Do not mark the task complete until the archive has been tested with both:

1. a first synchronization that changes files
2. a second identical synchronization that produces no tracked changes

Finish the requested project work.\\r\\n2. Run appropriate tests for that work.\\r\\n3. Capture or ingest the latest accessible conversation/session data.\\r\\n4. Run the chat synchronizer.\\r\\n5. Verify the manifest and changed transcript files.\\r\\n6. Run chat-sync tests or integrity validation.\\r\\n7. Determine whether transcript files actually changed.\\r\\n8. Commit and push chat changes only when appropriate.\\r\\n9. Report the synchronization result in the final task summary.\\r\\n\\r\\nDo not rely exclusively on a Git `post-commit` hook because prompts can finish without a code commit.\\r\\n\\r\\nWhere the Codex host exposes a legitimate task-completion hook, integrate the synchronizer there.\\r\\n\\r\\nWhere no reliable completion hook exists, make the `AGENTS.md` finalization instruction authoritative and provide an optional project task wrapper that runs synchronization before Codex reports completion.\\r\\n\\r\\nThe final Codex task response should contain a concise line similar to one of these:\\r\\n\\r\\n```text\\r\\nChat archive: 2 conversations added, 1 updated, 14 unchanged; committed and pushed.\\r\\n```\\r\\n\\r\\n```text\\r\\nChat archive: no transcript changes detected; no archive commit created.\\r\\n```\\r\\n\\r\\n```text\\r\\nChat archive: synchronization completed locally, but push was blocked because a possible secret was detected.\\r\\n```\\r\\n\\r\\nNever report success merely because the script was invoked. Confirm its exit status, resulting files, Git state, and push result.\\r\\n\\r\\n# Git Behavior\\r\\n\\r\\nThe transcript synchronizer must be extremely conservative with Git.\\r\\n\\r\\nIt must:\\r\\n\\r\\n* Detect the repository root.\\r\\n* Detect the current branch.\\r\\n* Verify the configured remote.\\r\\n* Fetch remote state before pushing.\\r\\n* Never force-push.\\r\\n* Never reset, clean, stash, checkout, or discard unrelated changes.\\r\\n* Never stage the entire repository with `git add .`.\\r\\n* Stage only files intentionally created or changed by the chat archive system.\\r\\n* Preserve unrelated staged and unstaged changes.\\r\\n* Detect merge or rebase states and avoid unsafe automation.\\r\\n* Use a lock to prevent concurrent synchronizations.\\r\\n* stop clearly when the remote branch cannot be updated safely.\\r\\n* retry only safe transient failures.\\r\\n* provide useful recovery instructions without modifying unrelated work.\\r\\n\\r\\nUse a commit message such as:\\r\\n\\r\\n```text\\r\\ndocs(chats): synchronize project conversations\\r\\n```\\r\\n\\r\\nIf the main Codex task already includes an intentional commit and the transcript changes logically belong with it, the transcript files may be included in that commit.\\r\\n\\r\\nOtherwise, create a separate transcript-only commit.\\r\\n\\r\\nDo not create a commit when:\\r\\n\\r\\n* no transcript content changed\\r\\n* only a local synchronization timestamp changed\\r\\n* the only difference is nondeterministic output\\r\\n* synchronization failed\\r\\n* the source was incomplete or untrusted\\r\\n* possible secrets require review\\r\\n\\r\\nAvoid rewriting `last_synchronized_at` in tracked files when no substantive transcript data changed. Otherwise every run would create meaningless Git noise, because humanity already has enough meaningless Git noise.\\r\\n\\r\\n# Atomicity and Reliability\\r\\n\\r\\nImplement:\\r\\n\\r\\n* atomic temporary-file replacement\\r\\n* UTF-8 validation\\r\\n* deterministic serialization\\r\\n* file locking\\r\\n* rollback of incomplete archive writes\\r\\n* clear nonzero exit codes\\r\\n* structured synchronization reports\\r\\n* idempotent repeated execution\\r\\n\\r\\nIf a crash occurs midway:\\r\\n\\r\\n* existing valid transcript files must remain valid\\r\\n* the manifest must remain valid\\r\\n* a subsequent run must recover safely\\r\\n* partially written temporary files must not be treated as archived conversations\\r\\n\\r\\n# Reporting\\r\\n\\r\\nCreate:\\r\\n\\r\\n`Codex_Chats/reports/latest-sync-report.json`\\r\\n\\r\\nThe report should include:\\r\\n\\r\\n* synchronization start and finish time\\r\\n* source types inspected\\r\\n* source coverage\\r\\n* conversations discovered\\r\\n* included\\r\\n* excluded\\r\\n* ambiguous\\r\\n* added\\r\\n* updated\\r\\n* renamed\\r\\n* unchanged\\r\\n* unavailable\\r\\n* redacted\\r\\n* failed\\r\\n* files changed\\r\\n* commit created\\r\\n* commit hash\\r\\n* push attempted\\r\\n* push result\\r\\n* warnings\\r\\n* errors\\r\\n\\r\\nAvoid changing the tracked report when it contains no substantive new information. Put highly volatile local execution diagnostics in an ignored cache or log instead.\\r\\n\\r\\n# README Documentation\\r\\n\\r\\nCreate a useful `Codex_Chats/README.md` explaining:\\r\\n\\r\\n* why the archive exists\\r\\n* what sources are supported\\r\\n* the limitation regarding inaccessible ChatGPT Project conversations\\r\\n* how automatic Codex-session synchronization works\\r\\n* how to request and import a ChatGPT data export\\r\\n* where to place `conversations.json` or the export ZIP\\r\\n* how conversations are filtered to this project\\r\\n* how updates and deduplication work\\r\\n* how hashes and stable IDs work\\r\\n* how secret redaction works\\r\\n* how to run a dry run\\r\\n* how to inspect ambiguous classifications\\r\\n* how automatic commits and pushes behave\\r\\n* how to disable automatic pushing\\r\\n* how to recover from a failed synchronization\\r\\n\\r\\nDo not describe functionality that has not actually been implemented and verified.\\r\\n\\r\\n# Tests\\r\\n\\r\\nAdd meaningful automated tests covering at least:\\r\\n\\r\\n1. First import creates a conversation.\\r\\n2. Reimporting the identical source makes no tracked changes.\\r\\n3. Adding a new message updates the existing file.\\r\\n4. any(part.startswith(\".\") for part in p.relative_to(path).parts))\n+        for candidate in candidates:\n+            yield from iter_chatgpt_path(candidate)\n+        for candidate in export_time = dt.datetime.fromtimestamp(path.stat().st_mtime, dt.timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec=\"seconds\").replace(\"+00:00\", \"Z\")\n+        try:\n+            with zipfile.ZipFile(path) as archive:\n+                for info in sorted(archive.infolist(), key=lambda i: i.filename):\n+                    pure = PurePosixPath(info.filename)\n+                    if info.is_dir() or pure.suffix.casefold() != \".json\" or info.file_size > 2_000_000_000:\n+                        continue\n+                    if pure.name != \"conversations.json\" and not re.fullmatch(r\"(?:conversation[-_]?\\d+|\\d+)\\.json\", pure.name, re.I):\n+                        continue\n+                    with archive.open(info) as stream:\n+                        try:\n+                            value = json.loads(stream.read().decode(\"utf-8-sig\"))\n+                        except (UnicodeError, json.JSONDecodeError) as exc:\n+                            raise SourceError(f\"Corrupt JSON member {info.filename} in {path.name}\") from exc\n+                    records = value if isinstance(value, list) else [value]\n+                    for raw in records:\n+                        if isinstance(raw, dict) and (\"mapping\" in raw or \"conversation_id\" in raw):\n+                            yield parse_chatgpt_conversation(raw, return\n+    if path.suffix.casefold() != \".json\":\n+        raise SourceError(f\"Unsupported transcript source: {path}\")\n+    source_hash = sha256_file(path)\n+    export_time = dt.datetime.fromtimestamp(path.stat().st_mtime, dt.timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec=\"seconds\").replace(\"+00:00\", \"Z\")\n+    with path.open(\"r\", encoding=\"utf-8-sig\") as stream:\n+        first = next((c for c in iter(lambda: stream.read(1), \"\") if not c.isspace()), \"\")\n+    values: Iterable[Any] = iter_json_array(path) if first == \"[\" else [load_json(path)]\n+    for value in \".codex\"))\n+\n+\n+def codex_titles(home: Path) -> dict[str, str]:\n+    result: dict[str, str] = {}\n+    path = home / \"session_index.jsonl\"\n+    if not path.exists():\n+        return messages: list[Message] = []\n+    created: str | None = None\n+    updated: str | None = None\n+    session_id: str | None = None\n+    try:\n+        with path.open(\"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as stream:\n+            for line_number, line in enumerate(stream, 1):\n+                if not line.strip():\n+                    continue\n+                try:\n+                    row = json.loads(line)\n+                except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:\n+                    # An actively appended final line may be incomplete; older corruption is unsafe.\n+                    if stream.read(1) == \"\":\n+                        break\n+                    raise SourceError(f\"Malformed Codex session {path.name} at line {line_number}\") from exc\n+                timestamp = \"assistant\"\n+                    text = str(payload.get(\"message\") or \"\")\n+                    messages.append(Message(role, text, timestamp, attachments=attachment_metadata(payload)))\n+                elif row.get(\"type\") == \"response_item\" and payload.get(\"type\") in {\"function_call\", \"custom_tool_call\"}:\n+                    name = str(payload.get(\"name\") or payload.get(\"tool_name\") or \"tool\")\n+                    arguments = payload.get(\"arguments\") or payload.get(\"input\") or \"\"\n+                    if not isinstance(arguments, str):\n+                        arguments = json.dumps(arguments, ensure_ascii=False, sort_keys=True)\n+                    messages.append(Message(\"tool_call\", canonical_text(arguments).rstrip(), timestamp, sha256_file(path))\n+\n+\n+def discover_codex_sessions() -> Iterator[Conversation]:\n+    home = codex_home()\n+    titles = codex_titles(home)\n+    seen: set[Path] = set()\n+    for directory in Conversation) -> str:\n+    return \"\\n\".join([conversation.title, *[m.text for m in conversation.messages]])\n+\n+\n+def classify(conversation: Conversation, config: dict[str, Any]) -> Classification:\n+    cid = conversation.conversation_id\n+    if cid in set(map(str, config.get(\"exclude_conversation_ids\", []))):\n+        return Classification(\"excluded\", [\"explicit exclude_conversation_ids override\"], \"Explicitly excluded by configuration\")\n+    if cid in set(map(str, config.get(\"include_conversation_ids\", []))):\n+        return Classification(\"included\", [\"explicit include_conversation_ids override\"], \"Explicitly included by configuration\")\n+    metadata = conversation.metadata\n+    flat_meta = json.dumps(metadata, ensure_ascii=False, sort_keys=True)\n+    flat_norm = flat_meta.casefold()\n+    evidence: list[str] = []\n+    for identifier in config.get(\"project_identifiers\", []) + config.get(\"repository_identifiers\", []):\n+        if str(identifier).casefold() in flat_norm:\n+            evidence.append(f\"metadata contains exact identifier: {identifier}\")\n+    if evidence:\n+        return Classification(\"included\", evidence, \"Exact project or repository metadata association\")\n+    paths: list[str] = []\n+    cwd = metadata.get(\"cwd\")\n+    if cwd:\n+        paths.append(str(cwd))\n+    roots = metadata.get(\"workspace_roots\") or []\n+    if isinstance(roots, list):\n+        paths.extend(map(str, roots))\n+    configured_paths = [normalize_path(p) for p in config.get(\"workspace_paths\", [])]\n+    for candidate in paths:\n+        normalized = normalize_path(candidate)\n+        for project_path in configured_paths:\n+            if normalized == project_path or normalized.startswith(project_path + \"/\") or project_path.startswith(normalized + \"/\"):\n+                return Classification(\"included\", [f\"workspace path association: {candidate}\"], \"Codex session workspace matches this project\")\n+    names = [str(x).casefold() for x in config.get(\"project_names\", [])]\n+    title = conversation.title.strip().casefold()\n+    if title in names:\n+        return Classification(\"included\", [f\"exact project name in title: {conversation.title}\"], \"Exact configured project name\")\n+    text = conversation_text(conversation).casefold()\n+    hits = [str(k) for k in config.get(\"project_keywords\", []) if str(k).casefold() in text]\n+    if len(hits) >= 2:\n+        return Classification(\"included\", [f\"distinctive project phrase: {h}\" for h in hits], \"Multiple distinctive project phrases agree\")\n+    if len(hits) == 1:\n+        return configured evidence\")\n+\n+\n+def filter_messages(conversation: Conversation, config: dict[str, Any]) -> list[Message]:\n+    result = []\n+    for message in conversation.messages:\n+        if render_body(title: str, messages: list[Message]) -> str:\n+    parts = [f\"# {title}\"]\n+    role_labels = {\"user\": \"User\", \"assistant\": \"Assistant\", \"tool_call\": \"Tool Call\", \"tool_result\": \"Tool Result\", \"tool\": \"Tool\"}\n+    for message in messages:\n+        label = role_labels.get(message.role, message.role.title())\n+        if message.name and message.role in {\"tool_call\", \"tool_result\", \"tool\"}:\n+            label += f\": {message.name}\"\n+        parts.extend([\"\", f\"## {label}\"])\n+        if message.timestamp:\n+            parts.extend([f\"**Timestamp:** {message.timestamp}\", \"\"])\n+        if message.text:\n+            parts.append(message.text.replace(\"\\x00\", \"�\"))\n+        if message.attachments:\n+           mime = str(item.get(\"type\", \"unknown\")).replace(\"\\n\", \" \")\n+                parts.append(f\"- `{filename}` ({mime})\")\n+    return canonical_text(\"\\n\".join(parts))\n+\n+\n+def render_markdown(conversation: Conversation, project_name: str, archived_at: str, enabled_redaction: bool) -> tuple[str, str, SecretScan, int]:\n+    messages = conversation.messages\n+    body = \"---\",\n+        f\"conversation_id: {yaml_quote(conversation.conversation_id)}\",\n+        f\"title: {yaml_quote(conversation.title)}\",\n+        f\"project: {yaml_quote(project_name)}\",\n+ return canonical_text(\"\\n\".join(header) + body), content_hash, scan, len(messages)\n+\n+\n+def empty_manifest(config: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:\n+    return {\n+        \"schema_version\": SCHEMA_VERSION,\n+        \"synchronizer_version\": VERSION,\n+        \"project_identity\": {\n+            \"name\": config[\"project_names\"][0],\n+            \"project_identifiers\":      \"total_conversation_count\": 0,\n+        \"total_message_count\": 0,\n+        \"source_coverage\": {},\n+        \"warnings\": [],\n+        \"migration_history\": [{\"schema_version\": SCHEMA_VERSION, \"synchronizer_version\": VERSION}],\n+        \"conversations\": [],\n+    }\n+\n+\n+def validate_manifest(manifest: dict[str, Any], repo: Path, check_files: bool = True) -> list[str]:\n+    errors: list[str] = []\n+    required_top = {\"schema_version\", \"synchronizer_version\", \"project_identity\", \"total_conversation_count\", \"total_message_count\", \"conversations\"}\n+    errors.extend(f\"missing manifest field: {key}\" for key in sorted(required_top - set(manifest)))\n+    records = manifest.get(\"conversations\", [])\n+    if not isinstance(records, list):\n+        return errors + [\"conversations must be an array\"]\n+    ids: set[str] = set()\n+    paths: set[str] = set()\n+    required_record = {\"conversation_id\", \"source_type\", \"source_identifier\", \"project_identifier\", \"title\", \"archive_path\", \"created_at\", \"updated_at\", \"first_archived_at\", \"last_synchronized_at\", \"message_count\", \"content_sha256\", \"source_sha256\", \"status\", \"redactions\"}\n+    for index, record in enumerate(records):\n+        if not isinstance(record, dict):\n+            errors.append(f\"conversation {index} is not an object\")\n+            continue\n+        errors.extend(f\"conversation {index} missing {key}\" for key in sorted(required_record - set(record)))\n+        cid = str(record.get(\"conversation_id\", \"\"))\n+        archive_path = str(record.get(\"archive_path\", \"\"))\n+        if cid in ids:\n+            errors.append(f\"duplicate conversation id: {cid}\")\n+        if archive_path in paths:\n+            errors.append(f\"duplicate archive path: {archive_path}\")\n+        ids.add(cid); paths.add(archive_path)\n+        if check_files and archive_path:\n+            path = repo / archive_path\n+            if not path.is_file():\n+                errors.append(f\"missing archive file: {archive_path}\")\n+            else:\n+                text = path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n+                match = re.match(r\"\\A---\\n.*?\\n---\\n\\n(.*)\\Z\", text, re.S)\n+                if not match or sha256_text(canonical_text(match.group(1))) != record.get(\"content_sha256\"):\n+                    errors.append(f\"content hash mismatch: {archive_path}\")\n+    if manifest.get(\"total_conversation_count\") != len(records):\n+        errors.append(\"total_conversation_count does not match records\")\n+    if manifest.get(\"total_message_count\") != sum(int(r.get(\"message_count\", 0)) for r in records if isinstance(r, dict)):\n+        errors.append(\"total_message_count does not match records\")\n+    return errors\n+\n+\n+def git(repo: Path, *args: str, check: bool = True, env: dict[str, str] | None = None) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:\n+    proc = subprocess.run([\"git\", \"-C\", str(repo), *args], text=True, capture_output=True, env=env)\n+    if check and proc.returncode:\n+        message = (proc.stderr or proc.stdout).strip().splitlines()\n+        raise GitSafetyError(message[-1] if message else f\"git {' '.join(args)} failed\")\n+    return proc\n+\n+\n+def ensure_git_safe(repo: Path, remote: str) -> str:\n+    git_dir = Path(git(repo, \"rev-parse\", \"--git-dir\").stdout.strip())\n+    if not git_dir.is_absolute():\n+        git_dir = repo / git_dir\n+    for marker in (\"MERGE_HEAD\", \"CHERRY_PICK_HEAD\", \"REVERT_HEAD\", \"rebase-merge\", \"rebase-apply\"):\n+        if (git_dir / marker).exists():\n+            raise GitSafetyError(f\"Git operation in progress ({marker}); archive automation stopped\")\n+    branch = git(repo, \"branch\", \"--show-current\").stdout.strip()\n+    if not branch:\n+        raise GitSafetyError(\"Detached HEAD; archive automation requires a branch\")\n+    if git(repo, \"remote\", \"get-url\", remote, check=False).returncode:\n+        raise GitSafetyError(f\"Configured remote does not exist: {remote}\")\n+    return branch\n+\n+\n+def commit_archive(repo: Path, files: list[str], config: dict[str, Any], push: bool) -> dict[str, Any]:\n+    result = {\"commit_created\": False, \"commit_hash\": None, \"push_attempted\": False, \"push_result\": \"not requested\"}\n+    if not files:\n+        return result\n+    branch = ensure_git_safe(repo, config[\"remote\"])\n+    existing_staged = set(git(repo, \"diff\", \"--cached\", \"--name-only\", \"-z\").stdout.split(\"\\0\")) - {\"\"}\n+    git(repo, \"add\", \"--\", *files)\n+    changed = git(repo, \"diff\", \"--cached\", \"--name-only\", \"--\", *files).stdout.splitlines()\n+    if not changed:\n+        return result\n+    # --only commits the archive pathspec while preserving unrelated staged entries.\n+    git(repo, \"commit\", \"--only\", \"-m\", COMMIT_MESSAGE, \"--\", *files)\n+    commit_hash = git(repo, \"rev-parse\", \"HEAD\").stdout.strip()\n+    result.update(commit_created=True, commit_hash=commit_hash)\n+    after_staged = set(git(repo, \"diff\", \"--cached\", \"--name-only\", \"-z\").stdout.split(\"\\0\")) - {\"\"}\n+    if not existing_staged.issubset(after_staged):\n+        raise GitSafetyError(\"Unrelated staged changes changed during archive commit\")\n+    if push:\n+        result[\"push_attempted\"] = True\n+        remote = config[\"remote\"]\n+        git(repo, \"fetch\", \"--no-tags\", remote, branch)\n+        remote_ref = f\"refs/remotes/{remote}/{branch}\"\n+        if git(repo, \"show-ref\", \"--verify\", \"--quiet\", remote_ref, check=False).returncode == 0:\n+            if git(repo, \"merge-base\", \"--is-ancestor\", remote_ref, \"HEAD\", check=False).returncode:\n+                raise GitSafetyError(f\"{remote}/{branch} is not an ancestor of local HEAD; pull/reconcile manually\")\n+        git(repo, \"push\", remote, f\"HEAD:refs/heads/{branch}\")\n+        remote_sha = git(repo, \"ls-remote\", remote, f\"refs/heads/{branch}\").stdout.split()\n+        if not remote_sha or remote_sha[0] != commit_hash:\n+            raise GitSafetyError(\"Push returned but remote SHA did not match the archive commit\")\n+        result[\"push_result\"] = f\"verified {remote}/{branch} at {commit_hash}\"\n+    return result\n+\n+\n+def report_signature(report: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:\n+    ignored = {\"started_at\", \"finished_at\", \"commit_created\", \"commit_hash\", \"push_attempted\", \"push_result\"}\n+    return {k: v for k, v in report.items() if k not in ignored}\n+\n+\n+def reconcile_duplicates(conversations: Iterable[Conversation], warnings: list[str]) -> list[Conversation]:\n+    chosen: dict[str, Conversation] = {}\n+    for item in conversations:\n+        previous = chosen.get(item.conversation_id)\n+        if previous is None:\n+            chosen[item.conversation_id] = item\n+            continue\n+        rank = (item.updated_at or \"\", len(item.messages), item.source_sha256)\n+        old_rank = (previous.updated_at or \"\", len(previous.messages), previous.source_sha256)\n+        if rank > old_rank:\n+            chosen[item.conversation_id] = item\n+        warnings.append(f\"Duplicate source record reconciled for {item.conversation_id}\")\n+    return [chosen[key] for key in sorted(chosen)]\n+\n+\n+def synchronize(repo: Path, config: dict[str, Any], sources: list[Path] | None, dry_run: bool = False, report_only: bool = False, no_push: bool = False, no_commit: bool = False, verbose: bool = False) -> tuple[dict[str, Any], list[str]]:\n+    started = utc_now()\n+    archive_rel = Path(config.get(\"archive_directory\", \"Codex_Chats\"))\n+    archive = repo / archive_rel\n+    manifest_path = archive / \"manifest.json\"\n+    old_manifest = load_json(manifest_path) if manifest_path.exists() else empty_manifest(config)\n+    old_records = {str(r[\"conversation_id\"]): r for r in old_manifest.get(\"conversations\", [])}\n+    warnings: list[str] = []\n+    errors: list[str] = []\n+    candidates: list[Conversation] = []\n+    inspected:        candidates.extend(discover_codex_sessions())\n+        inspected.append(f\"codex_session:{codex_home() / 'sessions'}\")\n+        for raw_directory in config.get(\"import_directories\", []):\n+            directory = repo / raw_directory\n+            if directory.exists():\n+                import_files = [p for p in directory.iterdir() if p.is_file() and p.name not in {\"README.md\", \".gitkeep\"} and p.suffix.casefold() in {\".json\", \".zip\"}]\n+                for source in sorted(import_files):\n+                    candidates.extend(iter_chatgpt_path(source))\n+                    inspected.append(f\"chatgpt_export:{source}\")\n+    candidates = reconcile_duplicates(candidates, warnings)\n+    report: dict[str, Any] = {\n+        \"schema_version\": SCHEMA_VERSION,\n+        \"synchronizer_version\": VERSION,\n+        \"started_at\": started,\n+        \"finished_at\": None,\n+        \"source_types_inspected\": sorted({x.split(\":\", 1)[0] for x in inspected}),\n+        \"source_coverage\": sorted(inspected),\n+        \"conversations_discovered\": len(candidates),\n+        \"included\": 0, \"excluded\": 0, \"ambiguous\": 0,\n+        \"added\": 0, \"updated\": 0, \"renamed\": 0, \"unchanged\": 0,\n+        \"unavailable\": 0, \"redacted\": 0, \"failed\": 0,\n+        \"files_changed\": [], \"ambiguous_candidates\": [],\n+        \"redaction_categories\": {}, \"suspected_secret_categories\": [],\n+        \"commit_created\": False, \"commit_hash\": None,\n+        \"push_attempted\": False, \"push_result\": \"not requested\",\n+        \"warnings\": These are legitimate local Codex records. It extracts exact visible user messages, visible assistant status/final messages, optional tool calls/results, timestamps, and available attachment names/types. It intentionally excludes developer/system instructions, token accounting, compacted memories, and private model reasoning. Thread titles come from the local Codex session index when available.\n+\n+It also reads official ChatGPT exports supplied by the user as:\n+\n+- `conversations.json` (incrementally decoded as a top-level array);\n+- a numbered conversation JSON file;\n+- an extracted export directory; or\n+- a ZIP read safely in place without extraction.\n+\n+Codex has no direct API here for live ChatGPT Project conversations. This workflow does not scrape browsers, cookies, tokens, credential stores, or protected ChatGPT data. A conversation is never fabricated from memory or a summary. Request a ChatGPT data export from ChatGPT's data controls, then place the JSON or ZIP in `Codex_Chats/imports/`. Raw full-account exports remain ignored by Git.\n+\n+For ChatGPT message trees, `current_node` is selected when valid and its parent chain is walked to the root. If it is unavailable, the synchronizer deterministically selects the leaf with the latest message creation time (then node ID) and walks that branch. Alternate branches are not merged, which avoids inventing an order.\n+\n+## Classification\n+\n+Classification is recorded as included, excluded, or ambiguous. Evidence is evaluated in this order:\n+\n+1. explicit conversation-ID include/exclude override;\n+2. exact project or repository identifier in metadata;\n+3. exact configured workspace-path association;\n+4. exact project name;\n+5. multiple distinctive configured project phrases.\n+\n+A single keyword is only ambiguous, never auto-archived. Generic words such as “treasure,” “pirates,” “website,” “Codex,” “PDF,” or “images” are not configured evidence. Inspect `ambiguous_candidates` in dry-run output or `reports/latest-sync-report.json`, verify the source manually, then add its stable ID to `include_conversation_ids` or `exclude_conversation_ids` in `.codex/chat-sync.json`.\n+\n+## Identity, updates, and format\n+\n+Original Codex/session or ChatGPT conversation IDs are preferred. When an export has no ID, a deterministic ID is derived from source type, source identifier, creation time, and the first user-message hash—never from the current time. The manifest retains the original archive path when a title changes, so renames cannot create duplicates. Different IDs remain separate even when titles match.\n+\n+Visible messages are normalized to UTF-8 with LF endings and insignificant trailing whitespace removed. The SHA-256 in each record covers the normalized Markdown body after redaction, not volatile front matter. Unchanged hashes do not rewrite transcripts, the manifest, or the tracked report. A partial or newer export never deletes an older archive record.\n+\n+Each transcript has YAML front matter followed by chronological `User`, `Assistant`, `Tool Call`, and `Tool Result` sections. Attachment metadata is listed without inventing attachment contents. `include_tool_output` can disable tools. `include_reasoning` is present for forward compatibility but hidden reasoning is never available to or written by this implementation.\n+\n+## Privacy and secrets\n+\n+Changed content is scanned before writing for private-key blocks, provider/API tokens, GitHub tokens, AWS keys, bearer tokens, credentialed database URLs, and explicit secret assignments. High-confidence values are replaced by labeled placeholders and only category counts enter reports. JWT-shaped low-confidence findings stop automatic commit/push for review rather than risking publication. Raw values are never written to reports, manifest metadata, or test snapshots.\n+\n+Review redacted transcripts and `redaction_categories`; never bypass an unresolved warning. Secret redaction is a defense-in-depth check, not permission to put sensitive account exports in Git.\n+\n+## Commands\n+\n+From any directory on Windows, the wrapper resolves the repository and prefers `.venv` or `venv`:\n+\n+```powershell\n+& \"<repo>\\scripts\\sync_codex_chats.ps1\" -DryRun\n+```\n+\n+From the repository:\n+\n+```powershell\n+python scripts/sync_codex_chats.py --dry-run\n+python scripts/sync_codex_chats.py --verbose\n+python scripts/sync_codex_chats.py --no-push\n+python scripts/sync_codex_chats.py --source C:\\path\\to\\conversations.json\n+python scripts/sync_codex_chats.py --report-only\n+python scripts/sync_codex_chats.py --validate\n+```\n+\n+`--dry-run` and `--report-only` do not modify the archive or Git. `--no-push` permits a local archive-only commit but suppresses the push. Normal mode writes atomically under a lock, validates the manifest and transcript hashes, commits only its explicit archive paths, fetches before pushing, refuses non-fast-forward or in-progress Git operations, never force-pushes, and verifies the remote SHA. It never resets, cleans, stashes, checks out, or stages the entire repository. Unrelated staged and unstaged changes are preserved.\n+\n+The tracked latest report changes only when transcript content changes. Volatile per-run diagnostics are stored in ignored `.codex/chat-sync-cache/`, preventing timestamp-only Git noise.\n+\n+## Automatic finalization and recovery\n+\n+`AGENTS.md` makes synchronization a mandatory Codex pre-final-response gate because the host exposes no version-controlled completion hook. The final response itself can only be ingested by the next run, when that same session ID is updated. This is an unavoidable ordering boundary, not a claim of live post-response access.\n+\n+If synchronization fails:\n+\n+1. read the sanitized error and `.codex/chat-sync-cache/last-run.json`;\n+2. resolve corrupt input, an ambiguous ID, a secret warning, a concurrent lock, an in-progress merge/rebase, or remote divergence without resetting unrelated work;\n+3. run `--dry-run`, then `--validate`;\n+4. rerun normally only after the condition is safe.\n+\n+Atomic same-directory temporary replacement and rollback protect existing files from ordinary write failures. Orphan `.tmp`/`.bak` files are ignored and never treated as archived records; the manifest remains authoritative.\n*** End Patch";
text(await tools.apply_patch(patch));
